Performance Targets Verification Report\\n\\n");\n        \n        let mut component_groups: HashMap<String, Vec<&PerformanceMeasurement>> = HashMap::new();\n        for measurement in &self.measurements {\n            component_groups\n                .entry(measurement.component.clone())\n                .or_insert_with(Vec::new)\n                .push(measurement);\n        }\n        \n        let mut total_measurements = 0;\n        let mut targets_met = 0;\n        \n        for (component, measurements) in component_groups.iter() {\n            report.push_str(&format!("## {}\\n\\n", component));\n            \n            for measurement in measurements {\n                total_measurements += 1;\n                if measurement.target_met {\n                    targets_met += 1;\n                }\n                \n                let status = if measurement.target_met { "✅ PASS" } else { "❌ FAIL" };\n                report.push_str(&format!(\n                    "{} - {}: {} (Target: {}, {:.1}%)\\n",\n                    status,\n                    measurement.operation,\n                    format_duration(measurement.measured_time),\n                    format_duration(measurement.target_time),\n                    measurement.percentage_of_target\n                ));\n            }\n            \n            report.push_str("\\n");\n        }\n        \n        let success_rate = (targets_met as f64 / total_measurements as f64) * 100.0;\n        report.push_str(&format!(\n            "## Summary\\n\\nTotal Measurements: {}\\nTargets Met: {}\\nSuccess Rate: {:.1}%\\n",\n            total_measurements, targets_met, success_rate\n        ));\n        \n        report\n    }\n\n    pub fn all_targets_met(&self) -> bool {\n file_path="src/performance/src/bottleneck_analyzer.rs">\n// Bottleneck Identification and Optimization Framework for SENTINEL Security System\n// Identifies performance bottlenecks and suggests optimizations\n\nuse std::collections::{HashMap, HashSet};\nuse std::time::{Duration, Instant};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n\n/// Bottleneck severity level\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Ord)]\npub enum BottleneckSeverity {\n    Low,\n    Medium,\n    High,\n    Critical,\n}\n\n/// Bottleneck type\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub enum BottleneckType {\n    CPU,\n    Memory,\n    I/O,\n    Network,\n    LockContention,\n    Algorithmic,\n    CacheMiss,\n    Database,\n}\n\n/// Bottleneck information\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Bottleneck {\n    pub component: String,\n    pub operation: String,\n    pub bottleneck_type: BottleneckType,\n    pub severity: BottleneckSeverity,\n    pub description: String,\n    pub current_value: f64,\n    pub threshold_value: f64,\n    pub impact: String,\n    pub suggested_optimizations: Vec<String>,\n}\n\n/// Performance profile data\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct PerformanceProfile {\n    pub component: String,\n    pub operation: String,\n    pub cpu_time: Duration,\n    pub wall_time: Duration,\n    pub memory_allocated: usize,\n    pub memory_peak: usize,\n    pub cache_hits: usize,\n    pub cache_misses: usize,\n    pub io_operations: usize,\n    pub network_bytes: usize,\n    pub lock_wait_time: Duration,\n}\n\n/// Bottleneck analyzer\npub struct BottleneckAnalyzer {\n    profiles: Vec<PerformanceProfile>,\n    bottlenecks: Vec<Bottleneck>,\n    thresholds: HashMap<String, f64>,\n}\n\nimpl BottleneckAnalyzer {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        let mut analyzer = Self {\n            profiles: Vec::new(),\n            bottlenecks: Vec::new(),\n            thresholds: Self::default_thresholds(),\n        };\n        analyzer\n    }\n\n    fn default_thresholds() -> HashMap<String, f64> {\n        let mut thresholds = HashMap::new();\n        \n        // CPU thresholds (percentage of wall time)\n        thresholds.insert("cpu_time_ratio".to_string(), 0.8);\n        \n        // Memory thresholds (MB)\n        thresholds.insert("memory_allocation_mb".to_string(), 100.0);\n        thresholds.insert("memory_peak_mb".to_string(), 500.0);\n        \n        // Cache thresholds (miss rate)\n        thresholds.insert("cache_miss_rate".to_string(), 0.1);\n        \n        // I/O thresholds (operations per second)\n        thresholds.insert("io_ops_per_sec".to_string(), 1000.0);\n        \n        // Lock contention thresholds (percentage of wall time)\n        thresholds.insert("lock_wait_ratio".to_string(), 0.1);\n        \n        thresholds\n    }\n\n    pub fn profile_operation<F>(&mut self, component: &str, operation: &str, f: F) -> PerformanceProfile\n    where\n        F: FnOnce(),\n    {\n        let start = Instant::now();\n        let cpu_start = self.get_cpu_time();\n        let memory_start = self.get_memory_usage();\n        \n        f();\n        \n        let wall_time = start.elapsed();\n        let cpu_time = self.get_cpu_time() - cpu_start;\n        let memory_end = self.get_memory_usage();\n        \n        PerformanceProfile {\n            component: component.to_string(),\n            operation: operation.to_string(),\n            cpu_time,\n            wall_time,\n            memory_allocated: memory_end - memory_start,\n            memory_peak: memory_end,\n            cache_hits: 0,\n            cache_misses: 0,\n            io_operations: 0,\n            network_bytes: 0,\n            lock_wait_time: Duration::ZERO,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn analyze_bottlenecks(&mut self) -> Vec<Bottleneck> {\n        self.bottlenecks.clear();\n        \n        for profile in &self.profiles {\n            self.analyze_cpu_bottlenecks(profile);\n            self.analyze_memory_bottlenecks(profile);\n            self.analyze_cache_bottlenecks(profile);\n            self.analyze_io_bottlenecks(profile);\n            self.analyze_lock_contention(profile);\n        }\n        \n        self.bottlenecks.sort_by(|a, b| {\n            b.severity.cmp(&a.severity)\n                .then_with(|| a.component.cmp(&b.component))\n        });\n        \n        self.bottlenecks.clone()\n    }\n\n    fn analyze_cpu_bottlenecks(&mut self, profile: &PerformanceProfile) {\n        let cpu_ratio = profile.cpu_time.as_nanos() as f64 / profile.wall_time.as_nanos() as f64;\n        let threshold = *self.thresholds.get("cpu_time_ratio").unwrap_or(&0.8);\n        \n        if cpu_ratio > threshold {\n            let severity = if cpu_ratio > 0.95 {\n                BottleneckSeverity::Critical\n            } else if cpu_ratio > 0.9 {\n                BottleneckSeverity::High\n            } else if cpu_ratio > 0.85 {\n                BottleneckSeverity::Medium\n            } else {\n                BottleneckSeverity::Low\n            };\n            \n            self.bottlenecks.push(Bottleneck {\n                component: profile.component.clone(),\n                operation: profile.operation.clone(),\n                bottleneck_type: BottleneckType::CPU,\n                severity,\n                description: format!(\n                    "High CPU usage: {:.1}% of wall time",\n                    cpu_ratio * 100.0\n                ),\n                current_value: cpu_ratio * 100.0,\n                threshold_value: threshold * 100.0,\n                impact: "Operation is CPU-bound, may cause system-wide slowdown".to_string(),\n                suggested_optimizations: vec![\n                    "Consider algorithmic optimizations".to_string(),\n                    "Use SIMD instructions for vector operations".to_string(),\n                    "Offload work to GPU/NPU if available".to_string(),\n                    "Implement caching for expensive computations".to_string(),\n                    "Use parallel processing for independent tasks".to_string(),\n                ],\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn analyze_memory_bottlenecks(&mut self, profile: &PerformanceProfile) {\n        let memory_mb = profile.memory_peak as f64 / (1024.0 * 1024.0);\n        let threshold = *self.thresholds.get("memory_peak_mb").unwrap_or(&500.0);\n        \n        if memory_mb > threshold {\n            let severity = if memory_mb > 1000.0 {\n                BottleneckSeverity::Critical\n            } else if memory_mb > 750.0 {\n                BottleneckSeverity::High\n            } else if memory_mb > 600.0 {\n    end_time,\n            duration_ns: end.as_nanos() as u64,\n            thread_id: self.thread_id,\n            metadata: HashMap::new(),\n        };\n        \n        let mut events = = Self::get_memory_usage();\n        \n        let mut metadata = HashMap::new();\n        metadata.insert("allocated_bytes".to_string(), (memory_after - memory_before).to_string());\n        \n {\n            let mut sorted = durations.clone();\n            sorted.sort();\n            \n            let total: u64 = durations.iter().sum();\n            let count = durations.len();\n            \n            stats.push(FunctionStats {\n                component: component.clone(),\n                operation: operation.clone(),\n                call_count: count,\n count as u64,\n                p50_duration_ns: sorted[sorted.len() / 2],\n                p95_duration_ns: sorted[(sorted.len() as f64 * 0.95) as usize],\n                p99_duration_ns: sorted[(sorted.len() as f64 * 0.99) as usize],\n            });\n        }\n        \n        stats.sort_by(|a, b| b.total_duration_ns.cmp(&a.total_duration_ns));\n        stats\n    }\n\n    pub fn operation: operation.clone(),\n                allocation_count: count,\n                total_allocated_bytes: total,\n                peak_allocated_bytes: peak,\n                avg_allocation_bytes: total / count as u64,\n            });\n        }\n        \n        stats.sort_by(|a, b| b.total_allocated_bytes.cmp(&a.total_allocated_bytes));\n        stats\n    }\n\n    pub               stat.call_count,\n                stat.total_duration_ns as f64 / 1_000_000.0,\n                stat.avg_duration_ns as f64 / 1_000_000.0,\n                stat.p95_duration_ns as f64 / report.push_str("|-----------|-----------|-------------|------------|-----------|----------|\\n");\n        \n        for stat in &memory_stats {\n            report.push_str(&format!(\n !self.enabled {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        let mut metrics = self.metrics.write().await;\n        metrics.push(metric);\n        \n        // Keep only last 10,000 metrics\n        if metrics.len() > 10_000 {\n            metrics.drain(0..metrics.len() - 10_000);\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn get_metrics(&self, component: &str, operation: Option<&str>) -> Vec<PerformanceMetrics> {\n        let metrics = self.metrics.read().await;\n        \n        if let Some(op) = operation {\n            metrics.iter()\n                .filter(|m| m.component == component && m.operation == op)\n                .cloned()\n                .collect()\n        } else {\n            metrics.iter()\n                .filter(|m| m.component == component)\n metrics.clone()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn get_summary(&self) -> PerformanceSummary {\n        let metrics = self.metrics.read().await;\n        \n        if metrics.is_empty() {\n            return \n        let mut durations: Vec<f64> = metrics.iter().map(|m| m.duration_ms).collect();\n        durations.sort();\n        \n        let p50 = durations[durations.len() / 2];\n        let p95 = durations[(durations.len() as f64 * 0.95) as usize];\n        let p99 = durations[(durations.len() as f64 * 0.99) as usize];\n        \n        let avg_cpu = metrics.iter().map(|m| metrics.iter().map(|m| m.cache_hit_rate).sum::<f64>() / metrics.len() as f64;\n        let total_errors = metrics.iter().map(|m| m.error_count).sum::<u64>();\n        let avg_throughput = metrics.iter().map(|m| m.throughput).sum::<f64>() / metrics.len() as f64;\n\n        PerformanceSummary {\n            total_metrics: metrics.len(),\n            avg_duration_ms: avg_duration,\n avg_cache_hit_rate: avg_cache_hit,\n            total_errors,\n            avg_throughput,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn get_component_summary(&self, component: &str) -> ComponentSummary {\n        let metrics = self.metrics.read().await;\n        let component_metrics: Vec<_> = metrics.iter()\n            .filter(|m| m.component == component)\n            .collect();\n        \n        if component_metrics.is_empty() {\n            return ComponentSummary::default();\n        }\n\n        let total_duration: f64 = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.duration_ms).sum();\n        let usize];\n        \n        let avg_cpu = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.cpu_usage_percent).sum::<f64>() / component_metrics.len() as f64;\n        let avg_memory = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.memory_usage_mb).sum::<f64>() / component_metrics.len() as f64;\n        let total_errors = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.error_count).sum::<u64>();\n        let avg_throughput = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.throughput).sum::<f64>() / component_metrics.len() as f64;\n\n        ComponentSummary {\n            component: component.to_string(),\n            total_metrics: component_metrics.len(),\n            avg_duration_ms: avg_duration,\n            p50_duration_ms: p50,\n            p95_duration_ms: p95,\n            p99_duration_ms: p99,\n            avg_cpu_usage_percent: avg_cpu,\n            avg_memory_usage_mb: avg_memory,\n            total_errors,\n            avg_throughput,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn generate_prometheus_metrics(&self) -> String {\n        let encoder = TextEncoder::new();\n        let metric_families = self.registry.gather();\n        let mut buffer = Vec::new();\n        \n Vec<ComponentSummary> {\n        let metrics = self.metrics.read().await;\n        let mut components: HashMap<String, Vec<&PerformanceMetrics>> = HashMap::new();\n        \n        for metric in metrics.iter() {\n            components.entry(metric.component.clone())\n                .or_insert_with(Vec::new)\n                .push(metric);\n        }\n        \n        components.into_iter()\n            .map(|(component, component_metrics)| {\n                let total_duration: f64 = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.duration_ms).sum();\n                let avg_duration = total_duration / component_metrics.len() as f64;\n                \n                let mut durations: Vec<f64> = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.duration_ms).collect();\n                durations.sort();\n                \n                let p50 = durations[durations.len() / 2];\n                let p95 = durations[(durations.len() as f64 * 0.95) as usize];\n                let p99 = durations[(durations.len() as f64 * 0.99) as usize];\n                \n                let avg_cpu = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.cpu_usage_percent).sum::<f64>() / component_metrics.len() as f64;\n                let avg_memory = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.memory_usage_mb).sum::<f64>() / component_metrics.len() as f64;\n                let total_errors = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.error_count).sum::<u64>();\n                let avg_throughput = component_metrics.iter().map(|m| m.throughput).sum::<f64>() / component_metrics.len() as f64;\n\n                ComponentSummary {\n                    component,\n                    total_metrics: component_metrics.len(),\n                    avg_duration_ms: avg_duration,\n                    p50_duration_ms: p50,\n                    p95_duration_ms: p95,\n                    p99_duration_ms: p99,\n                    avg_cpu_usage_percent: avg_cpu,\n                    avg_memory_usage_mb: avg_memory,\n                    total_errors,\n                    avg_throughput,\n                }\n            })\n            .collect()\n    }\n\n    fn                    <td class="status-good">✓</td>\n                        </tr>\n                    </table>\n                </div>"#,\n                summary.component,\n                summary.total_metrics,\n                summary.avg_duration_ms,\n                summary.p95_duration_ms,\n                summary.p99_duration_ms,\n                summary.avg_cpu_usage_percent,\n name) {\n            measure.enabled = true;\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(anyhow!("Measure not found: {}", name))\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn disable_measure(&self, name: &str) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut measures = self.measures.write().await;\n        if let Some(measure) = measures.iter_mut().find(|m| m.name == name) {\n            if measure.level == SecurityLevel::Critical {\n                return Err(anyhow!("Cannot disable critical measure: {}", name));\n            }\n            measure.enabled = false;\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(anyhow!("Measure not found: {}", name))\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn update_measure_status(&self, name: &str, status: ImplementationStatus) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut measures = self.measures.write().await;\n        if let Some(measure) = measures.iter_mut().find(|m| m.name == name) {\n            measure.status = status;\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(anyhow!("Measure not found: {}", name))\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn get_hardening_score(&self) -> HardeningScore {\n        let measures = self.measures.read().await;\n        \n        let total = measures.len();\n        let enabled = measures.iter().filter(|m| m.enabled).count();\n        let implemented = measures.iter().filter(|m| m.status == ImplementationStatus::Implemented || m.status == ImplementationStatus::Verified).count();\n        let verified = measures.iter().filter(|m| m.status == ImplementationStatus::Verified).count();\n        \n        let critical_measures: Vec<_> = measures.iter().filter(|m| m.level == SecurityLevel::Critical).collect();\n        let critical_enabled = critical_measures.iter().filter(|m| m.enabled).count();\n        \n        let score = if total > 0 {\n            (enabled as f64 / total as f64) * 100.0\n        } else {\n            0.0\n        };\n\n        HardeningScore {\n            total_measures: total,\n            enabled_measures: enabled,\n            implemented_measures: implemented,\n            verified_measures: verified,\n            critical_measures: critical_measures.len(),\n            critical_enabled: critical_enabled,\n            overall_score: score,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn generate_report(&self) -> String {\n        let score = self.get_hardening_score().await;\n        let measures = self.measures.read().await;\n        \n        let mut report = String::new();\n        report.push_str("# SENTINEL Security Hardening Report\\n\\n");\n        \n        // Overall score\n        report.push_str("## Overall Hardening Score\\n\\n");\n        report.push_str(&format!("**Score:** {:.1}%\\n\\n", score.overall_score));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- Total Measures: {}\\n", score.total_measures));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- Enabled: {} ({:.1}%)\\n", score.enabled_measures, (score.enabled_measures as f64 / score.total_measures as f64) * 100.0));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- Implemented: {} ({:.1}%)\\n", score.implemented_measures, (score.implemented_measures as f64 / score.total_measures as f64) * 100.0));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- Verified: {} ({:.1}%)\\n", score.verified_measures, (score.verified_measures as f64 / score.total_measures as f64) * 100.0));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- Critical Measures: {}/{} enabled\\n\\n", score.critical_enabled, score.critical_measures));\n        \n        // Measures by category\n        report.push_str("## Measures by Category\\n\\n");\n        \n        for category in &[HardeningCategory::Network, HardeningCategory::System, HardeningCategory::Application, \n                          HardeningCategory::Data, HardeningCategory::AccessControl, HardeningCategory::Encryption,\n                          HardeningCategory::Monitoring, HardeningCategory::Compliance] {\n            let category_measures: Vec<_> = measures.iter()\n                .filter(|m| m.category == *category)\n                .collect();\n            \n            if !category_measures.is_empty() {\n                report.push_str(&format!("### {:?}\\n\\n", category));\n                \n                for measure in category_measures {\n                    let status_icon = match measure.status {\n                        ImplementationStatus::NotImplemented => "❌",\n                        ImplementationStatus::PartiallyImplemented => "⚠️",\n                        ImplementationStatus::Implemented => "✅",\n                        ImplementationStatus::Verified => "✅✅",\n                    };\n                    \n                    let level_icon = match measure.level {\n                        SecurityLevel::Low => "🟢",\n                        SecurityLevel::Medium => "🟡",\n                        SecurityLevel::High => "🟠",\n                        SecurityLevel::Critical => "🔴",\n                    };\n                    \n                    report.push_str(&format!("{} {} {} - {}\\n", \n                        status_icon, level_icon, measure.name, measure.description));\n                }\n                \n                report.push_str("\\n");\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Compliance status\n        report.push_str("## Compliance Status\\n\\n");\n        for standard in &self.config.compliance_standards {\n            report.push_str(&format!("- {}: ✅ Compliant\\n", standard));\n        }\n        \n        report\n    }\n}\n\n/// Hardening score\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct HardeningScore {\n    pub total_measures: usize,\n    pub enabled_measures: usize,\n    pub implemented_measures: usize,\n    pub .filter(|v| v.severity == severity)\n            .cloned()\n            .collect()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn get_vulnerabilities_by_status(&self, status: VulnerabilityStatus) -> Vec<VulnerabilityFinding> {\n        let vulns = self.vulnerabilities.read().await;\n        vulns.iter()\n            .filter(|v| v.status == status)\n            .cloned()\n            .collect()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn update_vulnerability_status(&self, id: &str, status: VulnerabilityStatus) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut vulns = self.vulnerabilities.write().await;\n        if let Some(vuln) = vulns.iter_mut().find(|v| v.id == id) {\n            vuln.status = status;\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(anyhow!("Vulnerability not found: {}", id))\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn get_test_results(&self) -> Vec<PenTestResult> {\n        let tests = self.tests.read().await;\n        tests.clone()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn generate_report(&self) -> String {\n        let vulns = self.vulnerabilities.read().await;\n        let tests = self.tests.read().await;\n        \n        let mut report = String::new();\n        report.push_str("# SENTINEL Penetration Testing Report\\n\\n");\n        \n        // Executive summary\n        report.push_str("## Executive Summary\\n\\n");\n        \n        let total_vulns = vulns.len();\n        let critical = vulns.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Critical).count();\n        let high = vulns.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::High).count();\n        let medium = vulns.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Medium).count();\n        let low = vulns.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Low).count();\n        let info = vulns.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Info).count();\n        \n        report.push_str(&format!("**Total Vulnerabilities Found:** {}\\n\\n", total_vulns));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🔴 Critical: {}\\n", critical));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🟠 High: {}\\n", high));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🟡 Medium: {}\\n", medium));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🟢 Low: {}\\n", low));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🔵 Info: {}\\n\\n", info));\n        \n        // Risk score calculation\n        let risk_score = (critical as f64 * 10.0 + high as f64 * 7.0 + medium as f64 * 4.0 + low as f64 * 2.0) / (total_vulns as f64 + 1.0);\n        report.push_str(&format!("**Overall Risk Score:** {:.1}/10\\n\\n", risk_score));\n        \n        // Test results\n        report.push_str("## Test Results\\n\\n");\n        for test in tests.iter() {\n            report.push_str(&format!("### {} - {}\\n\\n", format!("{:?}", test.test_type), test.target));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Test ID:** {}\\n", test.test_id));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Duration:** {} seconds\\n", test.duration_seconds));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Vulnerabilities Found:** {}\\n\\n", test.summary.total_vulnerabilities));\n        }\n        \n        // Vulnerability details\n        report.push_str("## Vulnerability Details\\n\\n");\n        \n        for severity in &[VulnerabilitySeverity::Critical, VulnerabilitySeverity::High, \n                          VulnerabilitySeverity::Medium, VulnerabilitySeverity::Low, VulnerabilitySeverity::Info] {\n            let severity_vulns: Vec<_> = vulns.iter()\n                .filter(|v| v.severity == *severity)\n                .collect();\n            \n            if !severity_vulns.is_empty() {\n                report.push_str(&format!("### {:?} Vulnerabilities ({})\\n\\n", severity, severity_vulns.len()));\n                \n                for vuln in severity_vulns {\n                    let status_icon = match vuln.status {\n                        VulnerabilityStatus::Open => "🔴",\n                        VulnerabilityStatus::InProgress => "🟡",\n                        VulnerabilityStatus::Fixed => "🟢",\n                        VulnerabilityStatus::Verified => "✅",\n                        VulnerabilityStatus::FalsePositive => "⚪",\n                        VulnerabilityStatus::RiskAccepted => "⚠️",\n                    };\n                    \n                    report.push_str(&format!("#### {} {}\\n\\n", status_icon, vuln.title));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**ID:** {}\\n", vuln.id));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**CVSS Score:** {:.1}\\n", vuln.cvss_score.unwrap_or(0.0)));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Category:** {}\\n", vuln.category));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Affected Components:** {}\\n", vuln.affected_components.join(", ")));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Description:** {}\\n", vuln.description));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Remediation:** {}\\n", vuln.remediation));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**References:** {}\\n\\n", vuln.references.join(", ")));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Recommendations\n        report.push_str("## Recommendations\\n\\n");\n        report.push_str("1. **Immediate Actions (Critical/High):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Address all Critical and High severity vulnerabilities immediately\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Implement temporary mitigations while permanent fixes are developed\\n\\n");\n        \n        report.push_str("2. **Short-term Actions (Medium):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Address Medium severity vulnerabilities within 30 days\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Update security policies and procedures\\n\\n");\n        \n        report.push_str("3. **Long-term Actions (Low/Info):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Address Low and Info severity vulnerabilities in next release\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Implement continuous security monitoring\\n\\n");\n        \n        report.push_str("4. **Preventive Measures:**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Implement secure development lifecycle (SDLC)\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Conduct regular security training\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Perform regular penetration testing\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Implement automated security scanning\\n\\n");\n        \n        report\n    }\n\n    fn calculate_summary(&self, vulnerabilities: &[VulnerabilityFinding]) -> PenTestSummary {\n        let total = vulnerabilities.len();\n        let critical = vulnerabilities.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Critical).count();\n        let high = vulnerabilities.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::High).count();\n        let medium = vulnerabilities.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Medium).count();\n        let low = vulnerabilities.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Low).count();\n        let info = vulnerabilities.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Info).count();\n        \n        let risk_score = if total > 0 {\n            (critical as f64 * 10.0 + high as f64 * 7.0 + medium as f64 * 4.0 + low as f64 * 2.0) / total as f64\n        } else {\n            0.0\n        };\n        \n        PenTestSummary {\n            total_vulnerabilities: total,\n            critical_count: critical,\n            high_count: high,\n            medium_count: medium,\n            low_count: low,\n            info_count: info,\n            risk_score,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for PenetrationTestingFramework {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_network_penetration_test() {\n        let framework = PenetrationTestingFramework::new();\n        let result = framework.run_network_penetration_test("192.168.1.1").await.unwrap();\n        \n      report.push_str(&format!("- 🔵 Info: {}\\n\\n", info));\n        \n        // Scan results\n        report.push_str("## Scan Results\\n\\n");\n        for scan in scans.iter() {\n            report.push_str(&format!("### {} - {}\\n\\n", format!("{:?}", scan.scanner_type), scan.target));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Scan ID:** {}\\n", scan.scan_id));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Duration:** {} seconds\\n", scan.duration_seconds));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Coverage:** {:.1}%\\n", scan.summary.scan_coverage));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Vulnerabilities Found:** {}\\n\\n", scan.summary.total_vulnerabilities));\n        }\n        \n        // Vulnerability details\n        report.push_str("## Vulnerability Details\\n\\n");\n        \n        for severity in &[VulnerabilitySeverity::Critical, VulnerabilitySeverity::High, \n                          VulnerabilitySeverity::Medium, VulnerabilitySeverity::Low, VulnerabilitySeverity::Info] {\n            let severity_vulns: Vec<_> = vulns.iter()\n                .filter(|v| v.severity == *severity)\n                .collect();\n            \n            if !severity_vulns.is_empty() {\n                report.push_str(&format!("### {:?} Vulnerabilities ({})\\n\\n", severity, severity_vulns.len()));\n                \n     if let Some(cve) = &vuln.cve_id {\n                        report.push_str(&format!("**CVE:** {}\\n", cve));\n                    }\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**CVSS Score:** {:.1}\\n", vuln.cvss_score.unwrap_or(0.0)));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Source:** {:?}\\n", vuln.source));\n                    if let Some(package) = &vuln.affected_package {\n                        report.push_str(&format!("**Affected Package:** {}\\n", package));\n                    }\n                    if let Some(version) = &vuln.affected_version {\n                        report.push_str(&format!("**Affected Version:** {}\\n", version));\n                    }\n                    if let Some(fixed) = &vuln.fixed_version {\n                        report.push_str(&format!("**Fixed Version:** {}\\n", fixed));\n                    }\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Description:** {}\\n", vuln.description));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**References:** {}\\n\\n", vuln.references.join(", ")));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Recommendations\n        report.push_str("## Recommendations\\n\\n");\n        report.push_str("1. **Immediate Actions (Critical):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Update all packages with Critical vulnerabilities immediately\\n");\n with High vulnerabilities within 7 days\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Review and apply security patches\\n\\n");\n        \n        report.push_str("3. **Medium-term Actions (Medium):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Update packages with Medium vulnerabilities within 30 days\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Schedule regular dependency updates\\n\\n");\n        \n        report.push_str("4. **Long-term Actions (Low/Info):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Update packages with Low and Info vulnerabilities in next release\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Implement automated dependency scanning\\n\\n");\n        \n        report\n    }\n\n    fn calculate_summary(&self, vulnerabilities: &[Vulnerability], coverage: f64) -> ScanSummary {\n        let v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::High).count();\n        let medium = vulnerabilities.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Medium).count();\n        let low = vulnerabilities.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Low).count();\n        let info = vulnerabilities.iter().filter(|v| v.severity == VulnerabilitySeverity::Info).count();\n low,\n            info_count: info,\n            scan_coverage: coverage,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for VulnerabilityScanner {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n .collect()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn get_findings_by_status(&self, status: FindingStatus) -> Vec<AuditFinding> {\n        let findings = self.findings.read().await;\n        findings.iter()\n            .filter(|f| f.status == status)\n            .cloned()\n            .collect()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn update_finding_status(&self, id: &str, status: FindingStatus) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut findings = self.findings.write().await;\n        if let Some(finding) = findings.iter_mut().find(|f| f.id == id) {\n            finding.status = status;\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(anyhow!("Finding not found: {}", id))\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn get_audit_results(&self) -> Vec<AuditResult> {\n        let audits = self.audits.read().await;\n        audits.clone()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn generate_report(&self) -> String {\n        let findings = self.findings.read().await;\n        let audits = self.audits.read().await;\n        \n        let mut report = String::new();\n        report.push_str("# SENTINEL Security Audit Report\\n\\n");\n        \n        // Executive summary\n        report.push_str("## Executive Summary\\n\\n");\n        \n        let total_findings = findings.len();\n        let critical = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Critical).count();\n        let high = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::High).count();\n        let medium = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Medium).count();\n        let low = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Low).count();\n        let info = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Info).count();\n        \n        report.push_str(&format!("**Total Findings:** {}\\n\\n", total_findings));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🔴 Critical: {}\\n", critical));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🟠 High: {}\\n", high));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🟡 Medium: {}\\n", medium));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🟢 Low: {}\\n", low));\n        report.push_str(&format!("- 🔵 Info: {}\\n\\n", info));\n        \n        // Audit results\n        report.push_str("## Audit Results\\n\\n");\n        for audit in audits.iter() {\n            report.push_str(&format!("### {} - {}\\n\\n", format!("{:?}", audit.audit_type), audit.target));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Audit ID:** {}\\n", audit.audit_id));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Duration:** {} seconds\\n", audit.duration_seconds));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Compliance Score:** {:.1}%\\n", audit.summary.compliance_score));\n            report.push_str(&format!("**Findings:** {}\\n\\n", audit.summary.total_findings));\n        }\n        \n        // Finding details\n        report.push_str("## Finding Details\\n\\n");\n        \n        for severity in &[AuditSeverity::Critical, AuditSeverity::High, \n                          AuditSeverity::Medium, AuditSeverity::Low, AuditSeverity::Info] {\n            let severity_findings: Vec<_> = findings.iter()\n                .filter(|f| f.severity == *severity)\n                .collect();\n            \n            if !severity_findings.is_empty() {\n                report.push_str(&format!("### {:?} Findings ({})\\n\\n", severity, severity_findings.len()));\n                \n                for finding in severity_findings {\n                    let status_icon = match finding.status {\n                        FindingStatus::Open => "🔴",\n                        FindingStatus::InProgress => "🟡",\n                        FindingStatus::Resolved => "🟢",\n                        FindingStatus::Verified => "✅",\n                        FindingStatus::Accepted => "⚠️",\n                    };\n                    \n                    report.push_str(&format!("#### {} {}\\n\\n", status_icon, finding.title));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**ID:** {}\\n", finding.id));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Category:** {}\\n", finding.category));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Description:** {}\\n", finding.description));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Recommendation:** {}\\n", finding.recommendation));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Evidence:** {}\\n\\n", finding.evidence.join(", ")));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Recommendations\n        report.push_str("## Recommendations\\n\\n");\n        report.push_str("1. **Immediate Actions (Critical):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Address all Critical findings immediately\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Implement temporary mitigations while permanent fixes are developed\\n\\n");\n        \n        report.push_str("2. **Short-term Actions (High):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Address High findings within 7 days\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Update security policies and procedures\\n\\n");\n        \n        report.push_str("3. **Medium-term Actions (Medium):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Address Medium findings within 30 days\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Implement continuous monitoring\\n\\n");\n        \n        report.push_str("4. **Long-term Actions (Low/Info):**\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Address Low and Info findings in next release\\n");\n        report.push_str("   - Implement regular security audits\\n\\n");\n        \n        report\n    }\n\n    fn calculate_summary(&self, findings: &[AuditFinding]) -> AuditSummary {\n        let total = findings.len();\n        let critical = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Critical).count();\n        let high = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::High).count();\n        let medium = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Medium).count();\n        let low = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Low).count();\n        let info = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Info).count();\n        \n        let compliance_score = if total > 0 {\n            100.0 - ((critical as f64 * 25.0 + high as f64 * 15.0 + medium as f64 * 10.0 + low as f64 * 5.0) / total as f64)\n        } else {\n            100.0\n        };\n        \n        AuditSummary {\n            total_findings: total,\n            critical_count: critical,\n            high_count: high,\n            medium_count: medium,\n            low_count: low,\n            info_count: info,\n            compliance_score: compliance_score.max(0.0),\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn check_compliance(&self, audit_type: AuditType, findings: &[AuditFinding]) -> ComplianceStatus {\n        let critical_count = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::Critical).count();\n        let high_count = findings.iter().filter(|f| f.severity == AuditSeverity::High).count();\n        \n        let compliant = critical_count == 0 && high_count == 0;\n        let score = if findings.is_empty() {\n            100.0\n        } else {\n            100.0 - ((critical_count as f64 * 25.0 + high_count as f64 * 15.0) / findings.len() as f64)\n report.push_str(&format!("### {:?} Violations ({})\\n\\n", severity, severity_violations.len()));\n                \n                for violation in severity_violations {\n                    report.push_str(&format!("#### {} - {}\\n\\n", violation.file_path, violation.line_number));\n                    report.push_str(&format!("**Rule:** {}\\n", violation.rule_id));\n report.push_str(&format!("**Suggestion:** {}\\n\\n", violation.suggestion));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Recommendations\n        report.push_str("##
